msg:During the Chinese New Year, I want to put aside my daily life and find a hotel to enjoy life. Among the many hotels, I chose A.T. House, a light luxury hotel under Atour, which will open in 2021. It is relatively more novel and intelligent than some old-fashioned hotels.

üöó Transportation: There is no doubt about the geographical location. It is in the center of Xujiahui, about 150 meters away from Exit 1 of Xujiahui Metro Station (it will take some time to get down from the subway station to Exit 1). It is less than 10 minutes away from the Hong Kong Exchange and Metro City, which is convenient in general.

üîî Service: Attentive and thoughtful service, responsive to your needs, on call. On the night of the New Year's Eve, some desserts were arranged downstairs for everyone to watch the Spring Festival Gala together. In addition, people were sent to deliver dumplings and barbecued pork to the room (dedicated). On the first day of the new year, I also sent a small sachet, which is a small brain tiger üêØ (cute and lovely)

üì∫ Equipment: The room is full of smart homes, curtains, toilets, TVs, stereos, and Dyson hair dryers. If you choose a suite, there is a bathtub, coffee machine, refrigerator, and more complete equipment.

The room is probably turned on the central air conditioner, which is constant temperature, and I feel that there is no need to turn on the additional air conditioner. It just feels dry when I wake up in the morning.

Now the hotel stipulates that it does not take the initiative to provide a wash bag. If you don't bring a toothbrush and toothpaste, you need to ask the front desk for a wash bag when you check in.

The water in the bathroom is really big, the disadvantage is that it cannot be adjusted. In addition, the smart toilet is too smart. It will automatically open when it is close (such as washing hands), and it will automatically close after 1 minute. There may be advantages and disadvantages.

P.S. The hotel also has swimming pools, gyms, etc., but these venues are not open due to the Chinese New Year period.

üçÉ Environment: When you enter the lobby, it feels like a high tech hotel. The environment of the hotel and the room is good, very clean, and the color matching and decoration give you a comfortable feeling.

In addition, there is a cafe on the first floor (but not open for Chinese New Year), which should be very suitable for taking pictures :)

ü•ò Food: Originally, there was only one breakfast in one room, but the lady at the front desk helped to upgrade it to 2. The breakfast is semi-self-service, and you need to see the menu for the main dish. There are Chinese and Western dishes to choose from. The Chinese food includes yellow croaker wontons and some Chinese side dishes, while the western food includes eggs benedict and omlette and some western side dishes. Some other fruits, yogurt, bread, salads, etc. can be picked up by yourself. The amount is really enough, I can't finish it anyway.

btw, breakfast can also be delivered upstairs by a dining car, isn't it great!

I heard that afternoon tea is also good, if you have the opportunity, you can try it.

üè† Room type: The room I booked is the "Hollywood Room", 35-40 square meters, and there is only one Hollywood room on each floor. I chose a king-size bed (it's really big, of course, you can also choose 2 single beds), and the room prepared a basket of snacks (potato chips, popcorn, coconut flakes, soft drinks). My friend ordered the "Admiration Suite", which is 55-60 square meters. The room is prepared with two servings of fruit, red wine, white wine, beer, juice cola Evian water, etc. Relatively speaking, the Hollywood room is also enough. If you want a spacious one, of course, a suite is recommended. There are two TVs, a recliner sofa bathtub, and a large picture window.

üí∞ Price: Depending on the room type, the Spring Festival price will be 200-400 more expensive than usual. The Hollywood room is usually 900+ (1100+ for the Spring Festival), and the admiration suite is usually 1300+ (1600+ for the Spring Festival), which is also within a reasonable range.

The point is, during the two days of living, these snacks and drinks will be given a new one every day~

During the period, I broke a red wine glass and told the lady at the front desk that there was no additional compensation, but I always cared about whether we were injured or not, which was really considerate!

Anyway, it's a hotel worth staying in, it's definitely not a loss!

The room is intimately equipped with a steam iron, which is really easy to use, which is better than traditional ironing boards. The most easily missed and fun thing in the lobby is the piano painting installation in the elevator hall. Not only does it have music, but also randomly presents personal art paintings on the electronic screen. It is also fun to download to the mobile phone as a screensaver. There is also a magical conference table, which in turn is a ping-pong table. Remove the table top to create a billiard table. One table has three functions.
The breakfast is a semi-buffet style. The yellow croaker wonton in the set meal is really delicious, and the salted bean curd is also delicious. But the side dishes are average.
It was a bit unpleasant when I checked in, but Riesling at the front desk was very touched by the caring service. This is a brand new hotel. The team is mostly young and it is normal to make mistakes. This kind of caring service allows us to understand a young and vibrant service concept, which is very rare.
